<Review>A true jewel in the Turlock area! So glad that we found this spot for our daughter's wedding. A perfect combination of lovely garden grounds, Lavender farm and vintage charm, with original,  rustic buildings, dating back to when this was a  private homestead and working farm. The Bridal Cottage was once a hen house, which has been lovingly transformed into an accommodating, soft and pretty, vintage room where bridesmaids and bride can get ready while enjoying mimosas!

The Pageo staff was very accommodating and very easy to work with. Our daughter's Rustic-Vintage wedding was s dream, with vintage rentals provided by American Vintage Rentals...just look at the photos!</Review>< userid>

<user_id>109242534156499211276< /user_id><user_name>Olivia Hemenway< /user_name>< date>

<rate>5< /rate>< text>
I got married on July 21, 2018 at Pageo Lavender Farm in Turlock. After my husband and I got engaged, I started looking at outdoor garden and forest style venues in Northern California. After compiling a long list of options, I started prioritizing my favorites and emailing them for more information and options to come tour in person. Pageo was the second venue we toured in April 2017 and we fell in love with not just the scenery of the grounds, but the customer service we experienced. The next day we learned that a Saturday in July 2018 had become available and without a second thought about any other venue we had on our list, we signed the contract.

Holly was our primary point-of-contact throughout the period we were wedding planning. She was so friendly and responsive, never showing any impatience or frustration with the dozens of questions I probably emailed her about throughout that time. Whenever we came to visit the venue to work out more logistics, Josh always greeted us and got to know what we were envisioning for the day. Whenever we asked about how certain things could be done, there was never a ‚ÄúNo, we can‚Äôt do that,‚Äù but always a ‚ÄúLet us see how we can make that happen for you.‚Äù

About a month before, we were paired with our day-of coordinator, Jaimee Hinman. During our walkthrough we met with Jaimee in person and she was very well organized and knowledgeable about the wedding planning process, and gave us a few last minute suggestions around some planning items we were still handling. On our wedding day, everything went smoothly and I am so happy with how everything turned out! Our guests were blown away by the venue and service.

After planning my own wedding, I can say that I probably doubted almost every decision at some point in the process. But the one decision I never doubted for a second was booking Pageo Lavender Farm as our wedding venue. I cannot say enough good things out this place and these people!</text>

<Review>We just got married at Pageo (9/28/19!) The venue was absolutely perfect. Its was beautiful in the day time and at night! The string lights in literally every tree were stunning at night. The bridal sweet was massive. Plenty of space with good lighting to help the bridal party get ready. One concern we had with an outdoor venue was the uncertainty with the weather... But Pageo recently built a beautiful barn that they offered at no extra cost due to bad weather. That really eased our mind in case it rained on our day.

There was consistent communication with the venue months before and leading up to the wedding day to make sure all details were accounted for. Josh, Katie, Ana and the rest of the staff went above and beyond for us... from helping us find a DJ that fit our style to accommodating our last minute seating chart changes. Also, their vendor list is top notch. The catering, DJ, photographer were all from Pageo's vendor list and we could not have been more pleased with the quality of vendors they have.

They day of coordinator, Katie, provided by Pageo is amazing. Katie helped build and perfect our timeline for the wedding day. She was there early the day of to help coordinate with our vendors and make sure things were delivered and set up to our liking. She helped make our vision for the day come true!

Pageo also did not have any service fees or gratuity fees that a lot of venues in this area carry.

I would highly recommend Pageo!<//Review>< time>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
From our first tour and picnic lunch on the grounds to our big day, our experience with Pageo as our ceremony and reception venue was top-notch all around. Alexandria and the owners Patty and George were professional, communicative, detail-oriented, and kind. The care that they take in the business and the satisfaction of their clients is evident.

The venue itself is stunning and immaculate and perfect for a couple who values details and is looking for something more special than a banquet hall. Patty has conceptualized every inch of the property to make the space shine and has collected amazing antique items that just feel like they belong there without overdoing anything. It is not the "shabby chic" that tries too hard or a country style that not everyone can appreciate: it is pure sophistication with great pieces from the past. The many lights in the trees at night under the stars added so much to the atmosphere and were a better-than-expected surprise on our wedding day, which was the first time we had seen the venue at night.

George and Alexandria seem to keep the place running without a hitch and they were a pleasure to interface with intermittently throughout the year leading up to our wedding. George went above and beyond in helping to hang a chandelier for us and arranging our ceremony seats in an uncommon way to accommodate our unique processional for two brides. Alexandria addressed a couple of potentially problematic situations with professionalism and grace. At one point Alexandria came up to me to let me know that one of our guests was asking to purchase something from the gift store where our buffet had been set up and wanted to ask how I wanted to proceed. I was perfectly okay with it of course, but I thought it was so sweet of Alexandria to ask my permission for something that could potentially detract from the reason everyone was there and I respected her for thinking of that.

I could almost swear that George, Patty and Alexandria also made the weather better and brought some welcomed clouds and the breeze on what the forecast said would be scorcher of a day; our experience with Pageo was that great.< /review>

<Name>Deborah Hale<//Name><time>1494169779180</time><rating>5<//rating>< Text>
Although I have never had the opportunity (yet) to visit their lavender farm, I did find them selling their wares at the Turlock fair grounds. I love all things lavender and jasmine so I gave one of their testers a whirl. I ending up purchasing the lavender/jasmine lotion. A superb duo! I plan on heading back there next weekend for the spray. I love the lovely dark amber glass bottles their products are packaged in.  I do wish the owner would consider not putting dangerous parabens into the ingredient though. It is a lovely product and taking the parabens out would keep the product more 'natural'. I keep mine on the door in the refrigerator as it seems to make the product last longer. A tip I learned from another lavender farmer.<//Text>

< username>
Buckley Dueker</username>
< Text>
Great for a small shop! Good but small selection of hand picked retail releases at prices you'd expect. The staff picks are fun to look through and are interesting and eclectic. They are often playing some really interesting tunes as you browse. The staff is friendly and helpful, but I can't help but pick up a bit of that pretentious hipster vibe on occasion.

Used releases are in good condition but priced on the high side of collector value. You won't make a profit by buying and flipping from here, but it's a good place to find that first pressing you've been looking for at a reasonable market price.

Used vinyl in the dollar bins underneath has no organization, so be prepared to dig. Here is where you might find some gems. It won't be incredibly rare or valuable, but some of my favorite tracks have been found here and they're in relatively good condition.

My only complaint is that the reggae selection is seriously lacking, but that seems to be the case for both of the main vinyl sources in downtown Santa Cruz. I'm not sure why that is... I know it's a popular genre in the area.</Text>

Neat little store with a small collection of records.< /Text>
<user_id>107922499817866507384</user_id><user_name>Zo√´ Verdancii< /user_name></record></dataset><record>
< Time>
1424285290135</Time>
< Pictures>

< review>
This is my favorite record store. The staff is very knowledgeable and in no way pushy or in your face. The layout is simple yet expansive. There's an excellent selection of pristine new records, and a massive array of used records. The back wall holds the dollar bin, which in my eyes is the store's greatest asset. They get donations all the time from DJs and collectors, and don't have the time or man power to sort through and price each record. It's more cost efficient for them to just put it all on sale. Thus, you can find some truly exceptional stuff for a dollar. I've bought records of Miles Davis, John Coltrane, Freddy Hubbard, Guru, Company Flow, Talking Heads, Elvis Presley -- a wide array of true classics from every genre, some in near mint condition still in shrink wrap, for $1. You should shop here if you like music.<//review>

'21/3 1st time customer/review:
-- On the hunt for one product...tinted, SPF lip balm. Not carried in store at Walmart or Target; Walgreen's carried until they went under in 2020.
-- With above said, I entered a very well lit/clean store, was greeted by store security, and immediately greeted by perky sales associate asking if she could be of help. From there, I followed her around for five minutes while she attempted to locate what I was specifically looking for. Eureka, with dogged determination, she found it (the only type in entire, huge store...way down at practically ankle-high level on an end-cap shelf obscured by a shelf of the non-SPF product above it (see pic posted of Sun Bum product, comes in 4 tints) . Whew!
-- The cashier was as equally enjoyable/affable when ringing up the order.
-- Great eye contact and desire to engage customer from entrance to exit, plus huge/diverse selection in a clean/secure store gets 5 Stars.
-- Parking note: while Ulta is located in the eastern side-strip in a huge U-shapped shopping center, there are only four stalls right in front of the door/sidewalk--and three of those have now been designated (due to COVID) for curbside delivery. So, be prepared to walk from larger, central parking area which also crosses the one of two busy mall entrance roadways. Handicap parking, while on sidewalk side, is also much further down.< /Review>

<userid>102889352591729330688<//userid><user_name>Tiffany R.<//user_name><Date>1602964286495<//Date><rating>1<//rating><Review>I had an appointment booked with Michelle (salon manager) at 11:15am today, October 17th. I booked this appointment 6 days ago online. (Oct 11th)

I got multiple confirmations by text and on Ulta's booking website up to an hour before the appointment. I will attach photos. I took a screenshot of my confirmation just in case.

I'm glad I did. I got a call 20 minutes before my appointment from Michelle and this is how the conversation went:
"Hi this is Michelle from Ulta, you had an appointment at 11:15am?"
"Hi, Yes I did."
"I'm sorry, but the books have been glitching and booking appointments over each other. Can you move the appointment to 1pm today or 12:30pm tomorrow?"
"No, I'm sorry. I can't. I work a graveyard shift and have to go to sleep before a certain time. And I have a work event tomorrow all day."
"Oh okay. Thank you!"
"Thanks. Uh-"
I was going to ask if I still had my appointment at 11:15 but she hung up the phone before I could ask.

I went to my appointment, and a male hairdresser helped me at the counter. I said I had an appointment at 11:15 and he said I wasn't on the books. Michelle was at a station working with another girl. He asked who I booked with. I said Michelle and she came to the counter. I repeated that I was there for my appointment and when I tried to pull up my appointment online, it had suddenly vanished. Luckily I had the screenshot from an hour before and showed her. I don't think she was expecting that. She said "Oh I just spoke with you on the phone right? Yeah, I can't do the appointment. The books are weird and if you book online there's an issue. I can do your appointment at 1pm like I said on the phone."

Just to be clear, she never told me that she had literally canceled my appointment 20 minutes before I was supposed to arrive when she talked to me on the phone. Even if she had, that would be unacceptable as I booked this appointment 6 days ago and should have been notified far in advance of 20 minutes before my appointment that there was a booking issue.

I worked as a Guest Service associate at a waxing center for two years. I know exactly how online booking systems work, and I know that my appointment would have shown up in the system, even if it was double booked. Any well trained associate would contact these customers as soon as the issue was noticed. Michelle/Ulta had six days to handle this issue and notify me, and yet they didn't. Michelle was working on a dye job when I got there, and I can tell she waited until the very last minute to call me once she knew for sure she wouldn't be able to do my appointment. That is so incredibly inconsiderate.

She sneakily deleted my appointment off of the books 20 minutes before it was supposed to happen without telling me because she mismanaged her time, and just hoped I wouldn't show up. I have all of the proof in the screenshots I'm attaching to this review.

Even calling me an hour before would have been more polite. But no, I got called 20 minutes before, when I was already on the way there. This whole situation really ruined my day, as I haven't been able to cut my hair in over a year and I was so looking forward to my appointment today. I expect to hear back from management about this review. If I don't, I'll be calling the store's manager directly. I have proof of all of this happening the way I said it did in the screenshots. < text>
Sunny's Restaurant is one of the last TRULY GREAT Family Style, American Restaurants, that I know of in this area. I have been eating at Sunny's for (at least) 30 years (on & off) now. Over the years, I've had the pleasure not only of trying everything on the menu, at one time or another, but also of getting to know the Terrific service staff. In addition to the Waiters/Waitresses, it's been my honor to become good friends with the owners/founders of Sunny's, Andy & Cindy, as well as their kids (roughly my age) Summer & Shadow. Now for the Good Stuff‚Ñ¢:
THE FOOD-
All of the food served at Sunny's is prepared the Old-Fashioned way. For example, if you order a turkey sandwich, it's prepared with freshly (in-house) roasted turkey, carved straight off the bird. This style of fresh made food (never canned or frozen), carries through to all the dishes they make. I LOVE the Daily Specials, because they are usually -$2 Off the full menu price. On Monday, I ordered my FAVORITE Dinner, 1/2 Fried Chicken Dinner. The chicken is better than KFC, Popeye's, Church's, etc. Soup or Salad, Choice of Veg, Choice of Potato, Choice of Bread. All this for about $10.
I HIGHLY RECOMMEND Sunny's Restaurant to anyone with a Good Appetite!< /text>

<user>107030750642176652929<//user><user_name>M. Stephen Chase</user_name><Date>1489273336747< /Date>< rate>
4</rate>
< Text>
I eat here regularly and really enjoy this place. I've enjoyed Sunny's for about 10 years. Note-if you're looking for some hipster, fusion, happening place then this probably isn't for you. Sunny's is old school, diner, American food. The prices are reasonable and the food good, basic fare. Their portions are generous and the variety seems wide.

They have wonderful, hearty breakfasts and I have enjoyed everything I've ordered over the years although I'm partial to the Country Breakfast. They have daily dinner specials that are a good deal and seasonal specials, all of which are good deals and tasty food.

As for the staff, everyone I've encountered over the years has taken reasonably good care of us and, because I've eaten there over such a long period of time, they will recognize me and extend a warm welcome.

I agree that this is probably a place favored by a slightly older crowd and that's just fine with me. There are also families and a variety of ages that I've seen there too. I don't think I've seen any hipsters, though, so maybe not the place to go if you're looking for someplace trendy and hip.

Maybe one of the reasons for a preponderance of negative reviews on Google is the fact that the older people, and there are a bunch, who eat there aren't as familiar with social media, online review sites, and the importance of online reviews. They just now that they enjoy Sunny's and are probably okay that not everyone is as into the Sunny's experience like they are.

As for the decor, yeah, they could probably do with an update or refresh; however, as we all know, when that happens the ambiance, and some would say "charm" of the place would change, as well as the prices, undoubtedly. However, they entire center where Sunny's is located has undergone an exterior remodel/modernization that, as of this review, is nearly complete. Consequently, the outside is looking much cleaner and more modern but the interior is mostly unchanged.

I understand that people's experiences can vary widely in any service industry but I would encourage anyone who's thinking about eating at Sunny's to give it a try and come with an open mind. Don't let the haters discourage you; who knows, maybe you'll find the charm in this place as I have done. In a way, it's kind of like going back in time to when you could go to a neighborhood diner and just eat good food with friends.

Enjoy!<//Text>

<name>Kai Force<//name>< text>
This review is a little bit late in coming. The first time I walked in to Sunny's, I was about 11yo. In April, I'll be 43. OK, OK, A LOT LATE IN COMING. I thinks that it's difficult to right a fair review when you know people forever, but I'm gonna try.
1) The Food: This isn't the type of restaurant that you see every day (especially anymore). I'll explain. If you order a turkey sandwich, for example, they carve fresh turkey from the birds that they Freshly Roasted that day. Their soups are not "frozen in a bag" they a Freshly crafted by their talented kitchen staff.
This is how all restaurants used to be, or so I've been told.
2)The People: I'll try to be brief. The Zervos family has been in the restaurant business for an incredibly long time. Andy, the patriarch has run numerous restaurants in Orange County, even another Sunnys which used to be in South H.B. The Zervos family and their staff are more than mere restaurateurs. They are the people who remember your name. The ones who ask about family members, when they haven't seen them in too long. They are the people who sent home an order of soup, when they heard I was sick.
To sum it up, Andy, Cindy, their Children, and staff, are like family. It's like eating at your favorite aunt's house. It's being surrounded by people who care, and people you care about in return.
3)The Restaurant: Sunny's just completed a HUGE exterior renovation, and it couldn't look better outside. Haven't seen any noticeable changes inside yet, but I'm Certain that it is only a matter of time before they get to that also. I will be very honest, the interior is significantly dated in appearance. I know that can be a turn off to some people who are looking for the newest hippest spots. This isn't new or hip. It's Classic, a bit dated, and the food, service, and staff, are the BEST that you are likely to find, ANYWHERE in Orange County.< /text>
